guyde hope loue succour prouyde comming riuers side found hardly passable foote therefore still stood stound ne wist way foord mote pa thus whilest distressed case deuising doe nigh espyde armed knight approaching place faire lady lincked syde themselues prepard foord ride calepine saluting became besought courtesie neede safe conducting sickely dame perillous foord better heede take vp behinde vpon steed taunt returne perdy thou peasant knight mightst rightly reed full base euill borne would beare behinde burden scorne thou hast thy steed forlorne shame fare foote till thou another gayne let thy lady likewise doe beare thy backe pleasing payne proue thy manhood billowes vayne rude speach lady much displeased reproue yet could restrayne would owne palfrey haue eased pitty dame
